Zaidiyah memiliki pandangan yang lebih fleksibel dan moderat tentang imamah dibandingkan dengan Syiah Imamiyah (Itsna Asyariyah) dan Ismailiyah [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Mereka percaya bahwa Imamah harus dipegang oleh keturunan Ali dan Fatimah yang memiliki pengetahuan dan integritas moral [thesubmitters](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH7aHK9JTDa0zUSQrF_-Kz6rsOXZHrn3R2QzPKMeW2NCgcj17hNRDhvMwjcPG_oWbDhfPbNgN7qGrdJDXXa4ENgEC0JZA8JmK8D82I1b2EmlbcxYJ5WyIhR3Kk-KiaRp7QqBWOlQQ==). Tidak seperti Syiah lainnya, Zaidiyah tidak membatasi Imamah pada sejumlah pemimpin tertentu dan menerima kemungkinan beberapa keturunan yang memenuhi syarat mengklaim kepemimpinan [6]. Zaidiyah berpendapat bahwa Imam haruslah keturunan Nabi Muhammad yang paling berpengetahuan dalam ilmu agama [1]. Imam juga tidak harus tetap menjadi Imam seumur hidup [1] [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF7FNqciugjT5TKcJs83BpbjL04H-NUkD7woN1cKUIGlvXWA7hdKOhf0eu3tw5YrlM5pcLc1jP2gCa7zagdoJxvaC_zdZGwTtWi7h1Q4aQfZG1XvNZvCfZUgQd1m0xfEwXiSW_K6Q==). Zaidiyah tidak percaya pada kemaksuman imam mereka dan tidak menganggap mereka memiliki kualitas supranatural apa pun [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHrKeFiTZZUYIkProA_Hb_CNgR1BZ3qpABK8mGlClB1BwG5P09tZ4DXajKsvOtE0nl14_-XAIsrIDkgJO81VrzdPwbxCUoZBjQZ9vh-Y8THiQ-cWnQLzCKOSsIcI7yRkbH4).

*   **Syiah:** Al-Qur'an dan Sunnah, tetapi lebih menekankan pada riwayat-riwayat dari Ahlul Bait (keluarga Nabi) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Kitab-kitab hadis juga berbeda [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGDhRuIM6L0hWTT04CO9P_8myGYh1YNTUozOSXE8Bd0c-UAwQ81YnNUn7YQViABtIbhcLhRwW5ZUjBgnb_wb7Z6QbyvBpbxavvDQET7oA7GG25PM8D61Nrynq_w_KxSE1dLAE8XKDHy4_CytxL0PH9kk1D1ApHO-ar4UREcDfVQQgLeoiF2QLXBjENOP6oa-ELwaYFCjR7rabDJWaXheHX6totu85U=) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQG9W59mqQu5TC9h49_kr5U4pfh_Ffu4KoxzVvu-eNlHrxtQOI8y7yRHHEa_xiw9atXhgzOykKZ4gVvP9QY77uAtITRNu7445lt6XU7ul-fhnOHC7Z2FCSZ2hvIkFeBGQdzK5S96vqnHfVO7ptovpbzSLqk2noD6TK2CXPoqUw33MwWqIRXyxMU=) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI). Kitab-kitab utama Syiah ada empat: Al-Kaafi, Al-Istibshor, Man Laa Yah Dhuruhu Al Faqih, dan Att-Tahdziib [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Dalam doktrinnya, Zaidiyah lebih dekat dengan Sunni daripada Syiah lainnya [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF7FNqciugjT5TKcJs83BpbjL04H-NUkD7woN1cKUIGlvXWA7hdKOhf0eu3tw5YrlM5pcLc1jP2gCa7zagdoJxvaC_zdZGwTtWi7h1Q4aQfZG1XvNZvCfZUgQd1m0xfEwXiSW_K6Q==). Mereka memprioritaskan *ijtihad* (penalaran) dan *qiyas* (analogi) dalam jurisprudensi daripada kepatuhan dan mistisisme [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF7FNqciugjT5TKcJs83BpbjL04H-NUkD7woN1cKUIGlvXWA7hdKOhf0eu3tw5YrlM5pcLc1jP2gCa7zagdoJxvaC_zdZGwTtWi7h1Q4aQfZG1XvNZvCfZUgQd1m0xfEwXiSW_K6Q==).

**4. Praktik Ibadah:**

*   **Sunni:** Cara salat dan wudhu memiliki tata cara tersendiri yang telah dikenal luas.
*   **Syiah:** Terdapat perbedaan kecil dalam tata cara salat dan wudhu [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Syiah membolehkan nikah mut'ah (pernikahan sementara), yang dilarang dalam Sunni [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQG9W59mqQu5TC9h49_kr5U4pfh_Ffu4KoxzVvu-eNlHrxtQOI8y7yRHHEa_xiw9atXhgzOykKZ4gVvP9QY77uAtITRNu7445lt6XU7ul-fhnOHC7Z2FCSZ2hvIkFeBGQdzK5S96vqnHfVO7ptovpbzSLqk2noD6TK2CXPoqUw33MwWqIRXyxMU=).

**5. Teologi:**

*   **Sunni:** Rukun Iman ada 6 [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGDhRuIM6L0hWTT04CO9P_8myGYh1YNTUozOSXE8Bd0c-UAwQ81YnNUn7YQViABtIbhcLhRwW5ZUjBgnb_wb7Z6QbyvBpbxavvDQET7oA7GG25PM8D61Nrynq_w_KxSE1dLAE8XKDHy4_CytxL0PH9kk1D1ApHO-ar4UREcDfVQQgLeoiF2QLXBjENOP6oa-ELwaYFCjR7rabDJWaXheHX6totu85U=) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==).
*   **Syiah:** Rukun agama (*ushuluddin*) ada 5, yaitu Tauhid, Nubuwwah, Imamah, Al Adlu, Al Ma'ad [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGou8Ae0igIzWgVsOt8TpDIX8ZOrwoCNyYz1PjYOJMz8RmzEKDiQ4BGhdFinnNFdwQi6wleJ4wKAivBNLUrALDv_758cLSZvwz9wjJ9XtYOt-44z-ILRM-b9hMKBfsNNsPKbnOIbaRXuggdVocvbt-YiQtdsaiP5FkYaokB0435LLLGJQ==) [rewangrencang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH8C1icok6EPBavTBndGvz-5H5S-XZkh-sGceR-0n3vybnE8ovKyPl2pUVO2HV82qfN1G6l7oX7jqza0LPXQemXhI4V0kFyEDuFFNi5x2Yc2yyvWo7bIY1EIY1vu9r_8J0cautvEfWaMyOTfph8g6hH7FqcLGc50O2o9RJrpmwawHDGgco=).

**6. Al-Qur'an:**

*   **Sunni:** Meyakini Al-Qur'an yang ada saat ini adalah sama dengan yang diturunkan kepada Nabi Muhammad SAW [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==).
*   **Syiah:** Sebagian ulama Syiah meyakini bahwa Al-Qur'an mereka berbeda dengan Al-Qur'an Sunni, meskipun ada juga yang menyatakan sama (tetapi berbeda dalam penafsiran) [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGDhRuIM6L0hWTT04CO9P_8myGYh1YNTUozOSXE8Bd0c-UAwQ81YnNUn7YQViABtIbhcLhRwW5ZUjBgnb_wb7Z6QbyvBpbxavvDQET7oA7GG25PM8D61Nrynq_w_KxSE1dLAE8XKDHy4_CytxL0PH9kk1D1ApHO-ar4UREcDfVQQgLeoiF2QLXBjENOP6oa-ELwaYFCjR7rabDJWaXheHX6totu85U=) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI).

**7. Raj'ah (Kebangkitan Kembali):**

*   **Sunni:** Tidak ada dalam ajaran Ahlussunnah [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI).
*   **Syiah:** Raj'ah adalah salah satu aqidah Syiah, di mana di akhir zaman, Imam Mahdi akan keluar dan ahlul bait akan membalas dendam kepada musuh-musuhnya [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Zaidiyah tidak meyakini Imam Ghaib yang akan datang kembali seperti yang diyakini oleh Syiah Itsna Asyariyah [suaraislam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFmP88-rpL1neCRPRF3GqG1HE8sLxII8U44PJ01F_pKffmF6bqhgDM0gciBUBtnGGnOfUZ6jCDLkh0RJwns2vXnCcXgjwFziF_nevBbZGZw7drZ0BTng3A2JLUNV1Y0iQPYWM01HmEU-8MO).

**8. Taqiyah (Menyembunyikan Keyakinan):**

*   **Syiah:** Diperbolehkan menyembunyikan keyakinan untuk melindungi diri [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Zaidiyah, umumnya, menolak *taqiyah* [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGtFP9P05wY6G4hh69C2zLutWalSzgjMGoGJ-dstm_-WzkKnBK0qZZ4Hhn39xLc9oGn1cN7BLTEZ-_onqkKTIEvhqYDIN5wqspOBKZRKb3zqNol0oOR5jpGEB2DCzAjDf7n3B3_qOja9fDto8QdWNS1Wgg=). Sementara itu, bagi  Ithna Ashariyah, *taqiyah* adalah salah satu prinsip dasar dan dianggap wajib sampai imam yang tersembunyi muncul [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGInp7C8N1hwkkl2eJ5MoyFgCzV-oNlVlBnMKC0iEucWBiazlK6CQqlnmlPahZ0UhmZALwC4wQRE4jW1lmUdCcWElhVdDe0Tqt62HTlqml7Z5FSSxxQAhQ43uAC-MVpIXF-) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHX1Y7hmT4vI_tuGQJeFTsmuiq6ne8oUBsXyjHej3RJqbaxIVEyNIlf5cKhrAhKICaojjp1d-FbmgNbOoIgdEvPH9z0lZVXVc3WG-O0w9_IBNziRyR64akEvyYKq5N5Phz8Apk-B7Ut15dh3PNbZe3S7QmIN8-UwGfy8ytsANY6yNDnbixjbhq-fr4wuUvkjg==).

**9. Pandangan Terhadap Pemimpin yang Tidak Adil dan Konsep *Khuruj*:**

*   **Zaidiyah:** Memandang bolehnya memberontak terhadap pemimpin yang jahat [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Ini adalah inti dari konsep *khuruj*. Zaydis percaya bahwa seorang Imam sejati harus berjuang melawan penguasa yang korup [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHTFVjjrTzI1FmKuoihOLXnGvJ7vShVzXXwUjN2Fi3UcGggevIxvy6ZBgRejRUiyOzNBCCNtDwY5XJypE1veEe79HmL9MSFx_HCzhHE1RguF5aKCftrfxBhqJ73hYk08_RUbmttTC0tvPDhXnIgnehoDu1WUcs4) [redzambala](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHk2m32VMkJMa3KWeoQP-GZ2TY6Vk50sTN-ip-P4KJ2MtmG4PHeUGo4V03jq1YJA1213ob9im2D4Oj9oYRpPpSnTys2EPJ2-alLwZ2aGkFdAa-QgAYoNQBj-3mJjP3MrqRwZGa3s3_JA6yXXj8J5djqL7w=) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQE7lDs8s5XQQQpkxbk06sYIwuIZZh7vwXDWe9HpSgVnmSQ8_VSC7dcx07TOPlVr4lofeq3vUOsFiVQgeexOJgdiINK9sMZxJfY-q2Htx2C8wTsErbXYY3koz1ZTZSMmIrQ=). Pemberontakan melawan penguasa yang tidak adil menjadi kualifikasi utama bagi setiap pemimpin spiritual-politik yang sah dalam Zaydism [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHTFVjjrTzI1FmKuoihOLXnGvJ7vShVzXXwUjN2Fi3UcGggevIxvy6ZBgRejRUiyOzNBCCNtDwY5XJypE1veEe79HmL9MSFx_HCzhHE1RguF5aKCftrfxBhqJ73hYk08_RUbmttTC0tvPDhXnIgnehoDu1WUcs4) [washingtoninstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFtLmeY78mTVFzCYF9e-wjxIPGNRttxrEnesYpwP03HtRxl-2DOl1uGPLL7aqv4I7zz8jQ0vAekLuIqf7eSnSzbadXo6Jedm2Sig5sZPV7MPu4WnKxFyCUz4wkR2I1bsWxYc0k3s84YwTRSzwJwikUF6TmOH0LoXXe4HB-CTW_xzanUUONV7UD_oa9oh4wsWnKFyfA6Sw==). Sejak pertengahan abad ke-20, ulama Zaidiyah menafsirkan *khuruj* sebagai partisipasi dalam politik elektoral [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF7FNqciugjT5TKcJs83BpbjL04H-NUkD7woN1cKUIGlvXWA7hdKOhf0eu3tw5YrlM5pcLc1jP2gCa7zagdoJxvaC_zdZGwTtWi7h1Q4aQfZG1XvNZvCfZUgQd1m0xfEwXiSW_K6Q==).

**Sejarah dan Perkembangan Syiah Zaidiyah:**

Syiah Zaidiyah muncul pada abad ke-8 Masehi, mengikuti ajaran Zayd bin Ali [1, 6]. Zayd bin Ali dikenal sebagai seorang alim yang saleh dan pemberani yang melakukan pemberontakan melawan kekhalifahan Umayyah yang dianggapnya tiran dan korup [2, 6]. Zaidiyah memiliki sejarah panjang di Yaman dan memainkan peran penting dalam lanskap politik negara tersebut [5, 6] [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFxZYDVkQ9XT328mO_-xJeJo1iqAsh_uB0-gRcLCHsvUhM-xsp8qZWGJkmi54Rf1gai2DJYb4tIoBHdXTHCcHeYl6xFyL0aI3Itc3eSDrc87o3qgkUjqSTN-8poTVYuit0Yix9R4Waz74k2ohqejZgh90u2FFYJCz_CwmucVDInje7fnDBRDsfuTkbTxyPBTLKecFf0MnuK9tehPXvC41kT_ixoXKRFmJ2rJTjMRPQdpMxUYaplqMM=) [thesubmitters](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH7aHK9JTDa0zUSQrF_-Kz6rsOXZHrn3R2QzPKMeW2NCgcj17hNRDhvMwjcPG_oWbDhfPbNgN7qGrdJDXXa4ENgEC0JZA8JmK8D82I1b2EmlbcxYJ5WyIhR3Kk-KiaRp7QqBWOlQQ==).

**Sejarah dan Perkembangan Syiah Itsna Asyariyah:**

Pada awal abad ke-16, berdirinya Kerajaan Safawi di Iran menandai perubahan penting [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQEKYz28Z5PAZPLQIzpRzT0iH3cBS9cR9b8dXX0N8MJ6r7YvRS4UnSb7batBzFFADqpf_dyWuvDEbg9NSKo1VUHalu8dTRsnN_lLexCfHX77nUiEDmLBkqWsixngSHC1cdv67tu7Ycu2J_x3GE7w7q1BJ1fdWx2oSjstlZJDhsB6AEnQVLh5T9B3ER_tM1eQks8CzhZUH55-PWxfFHOTWlIuj2F5pgJv6jExZ2jOkoOs7LnYfp05zmYBsso=). Shah Ismail I menjadikan Syiah Itsna Asyariyah sebagai keyakinan resmi kerajaan [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQER30xoRAolCOcmex9bzWgS8XaV7L3ZYM_Jdl63onH9xZyQBZIpXGszdoGgCUX9l-o51nzyp3F-tIIEUAzl0cb-8z_E5eulCZxTthM-1vZA2ZYfRQ2MggvWEL20LVuxWu67jR5G7n-I2-2T5PWu-z6oan5cHfOgChIYCcVi8AbPppvHhaJ-yRxE4qsL6lZv8TjJWBl9e67sm--5ZqdILRRPTr3s6vhW6SV7).

Penting untuk diingat bahwa perbedaan-perbedaan ini seringkali menjadi sumber ketegangan antara Sunni dan Syiah [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Ada upaya-upaya rekonsiliasi dan dialog antar-mazhab untuk mengurangi konflik dan meningkatkan saling pengertian [rumahfiqih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFOVjw38SZuwyjs67bXU4t2q7XWqxmSgvPyHOcQjKse1YIjxTCxNxrywvRNUWwrZMd70JcQ2JDu_NLayc9eW0Cu0NG3JQZ-dng2ngsyGVDsTuUa48k_EtYa370geM6z-Wr3jk08oQ==) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [iaisambas](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGiyMp9uJSLV-vfjY0cpLRMDXgxFcSL-xmhI49kEFRX2_7SWwSR2Nr9G6zOyCBKxiylGfrsvXteRJ7YjXrP-YAgGrdlaLkYLPCNZvcWkcn4uwQRDZA6Gf-OeLQ6TUzskM-sUijuSfHljfcBcrnrxLpP_4DRjNwgdytbZy4OzGsxfHWNSy5Z6k377V1AmppJhdUm0w==). Dalam tubuh Syiah pun terdapat banyak sekte dengan perbedaan pandangan [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Tidak semua kelompok Syiah memiliki pandangan yang sama [rumahfiqih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFOVjw38SZuwyjs67bXU4t2q7XWqxmSgvPyHOcQjKse1YIjxTCxNxrywvRNUWwrZMd70JcQ2JDu_NLayc9eW0Cu0NG3JQZ-dng2ngsyGVDsTuUa48k_EtYa370geM6z-Wr3jk08oQ==) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Sebagian besar umat Islam (termasuk Sunni dan Syiah) mengucapkan dua kalimat syahadat, meyakini Al-Qur'an sebagai sumber syariat Islam, dan menghadap kiblat yang sama saat salat [mushafjournal](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==0).

SEARCH QUERIES USED
----------------------------------------
1. perbedaan utama syiah zaidi itsna asyari dan sunni
2. sejarah dan doktrin syiah zaidi
3. sejarah dan doktrin syiah itsna asyari
4. What are the specific legal and theological justifications used by Zaidiyah scholars for the concept of 'khuruj' (rebellion against unjust rulers), and how have these justifications been applied in historical contexts, particularly in Yemen?
5. What are the key differences in the interpretation and application of 'Taqiyah' (dissimulation) between Shia Zaidiyah and Shia Ithna Ashariyah, and how do these differences manifest in their respective legal and social practices?

--- Research Result 1 ---
Tentu, berikut adalah perbedaan utama antara Syiah Zaidiyah, Itsna Asyariyah, dan Sunni, yang disarikan dari berbagai sumber:

**1. [uin-malang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Kepemimpinan (Imamah):**

*   **Sunni:** Kepemimpinan didasarkan pada musyawarah dan kesepakatan umat. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [iaisambas](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2) Pemilihan pemimpin dilakukan oleh dewan pemilihan (ahl al-ikhtiyar/ahlul aqdi wal halli). [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Khalifah (imam) adalah manusia biasa yang tidak memiliki sifat ma'shum (terjaga dari dosa). [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
*   **Syiah Itsna Asyariyah:** Imamah adalah bagian dari ushuluddin (pokok agama) dan merupakan rukun iman. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3) Imam harus dari keturunan Ali bin Abi Thalib dan Fatimah, dipilih melalui nash (penunjukan) oleh Nabi, dan memiliki sifat ma'shum (seperti para nabi). [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Mereka meyakini 12 imam. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3)
*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:**  Menekankan legitimasi keturunan Ali bin Abi Thalib sebagai pemimpin, tetapi tidak seketat Itsna Asyariyah dalam hal kriteria imam. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Zaidiyah memiliki pandangan yang lebih fleksibel dan moderat tentang imamah dibandingkan dengan Syiah Imamiyah (Itsna Asyariyah) dan Ismailiyah. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)

**2. [uin-malang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Pandangan terhadap Sahabat Nabi:**

*   **Sunni:** Semua sahabat Nabi dianggap adil dan dapat dipercaya riwayatnya.
*   **Syiah Itsna Asyariyah:** Beberapa sahabat dianggap murtad setelah wafatnya Nabi karena membai'at Abu Bakar sebagai khalifah. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) Syiah diperkenankan mencaci-maki sahabat. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4)
*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Memiliki pandangan yang lebih lunak terhadap para sahabat. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-5) Imam Zaid bin Ali menolak mencela Abu Bakar dan Umar, bahkan memuji mereka. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-5)

**3. [uin-malang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Sumber Hukum:**

*   **Sunni:** Al-Qur'an dan Sunnah Nabi (yang diriwayatkan oleh para sahabat secara luas) adalah sumber hukum utama. [detik](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-6) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
*   **Syiah:** Al-Qur'an dan Sunnah, tetapi lebih menekankan pada riwayat-riwayat dari Ahlul Bait (keluarga Nabi). [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Kitab-kitab hadis juga berbeda. [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4)

**4. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3) Praktik Ibadah:**

*   **Sunni:** Cara salat dan wudhu memiliki tata cara tersendiri yang telah dikenal luas.
*   **Syiah:** Terdapat perbedaan kecil dalam tata cara salat dan wudhu. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
*   **Syiah:** Membolehkan nikah mut'ah (pernikahan sementara), yang dilarang dalam Sunni. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8)

**5. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Teologi:**

*   **Sunni:** Rukun Iman ada 6. [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
*   **Syiah:** Rukun agama (ushuluddin) ada 5, yaitu Tauhid, Nubuwwah, Imamah, Al Adlu, Al Ma'ad. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)

**6. [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Kitab Utama:**

*   **Sunni:** Kitab-kitab hadis utama adalah Shahih Bukhari, Shahih Muslim, dan lainnya. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-8) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
*   **Syiah:** Kitab-kitab utama Syiah ada empat: Al-Kaafi, Al-Istibshor, Man Laa Yah Dhuruhu Al Faqih, dan Att-Tahdziib. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)

**7. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Konsep Imamah dalam Ushuluddin:**

*   **Sunni:** Masalah Imamah terkait dengan keduniaan dan bukan bagian penting dari hukum Islam. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3)
*   **Syiah Itsna Asyariyah:** Imamah adalah bagian dari ushuluddin (pokok agama) dan merupakan rukun iman. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-3)

**8. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Al-Qur'an:**

*   **Sunni:** Meyakini Al-Qur'an yang ada saat ini adalah sama dengan yang diturunkan kepada Nabi Muhammad SAW. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
*   **Syiah:** Sebagian ulama Syiah meyakini bahwa Al-Qur'an mereka berbeda dengan Al-Qur'an Sunni, meskipun ada juga yang menyatakan sama (tetapi berbeda dalam penafsiran). [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-7) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4)

**9. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Raj'ah (Kebangkitan Kembali):**

*   **Sunni:** Tidak ada dalam ajaran Ahlussunnah. [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4)
*   **Syiah:** Raj'ah adalah salah satu aqidah Syiah, di mana di akhir zaman, Imam Mahdi akan keluar dan ahlul bait akan membalas dendam kepada musuh-musuhnya. [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)

**10. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Taqiyah (Menyembunyikan Keyakinan):**

*   **Syiah:** Diperbolehkan menyembunyikan keyakinan untuk melindungi diri.

**11. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [uin-malang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-0) Pandangan Terhadap Pemimpin yang Tidak Adil:**

*   **Zaidiyah:** Memandang bolehnya memberontak terhadap pemimpin yang jahat. [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-4) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)

**Penting untuk dicatat:**

*   Perbedaan-perbedaan ini seringkali menjadi sumber ketegangan antara Sunni dan Syiah. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
*   Ada upaya-upaya rekonsiliasi dan dialog antar-mazhab untuk mengurangi konflik dan meningkatkan saling pengertian. [rumahfiqih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) [iaisambas](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-2)
*   Dalam tubuh Syiah pun terdapat banyak sekte dengan perbedaan pandangan. [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1) Tidak semua kelompok Syiah memiliki pandangan yang sama. [rumahfiqih](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-9) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-1)
*   Sebagian besar umat Islam (termasuk Sunni dan Syiah) mengucapkan dua kalimat syahadat, meyakini Al-Qur'an sebagai sumber syariat Islam, dan menghadap kiblat yang sama saat salat. [mushafjournal](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/0-10)


--- Research Result 2 ---
Berdasarkan hasil pencarian, berikut adalah rangkuman mengenai sejarah dan doktrin Syiah Zaidiyah:

**Sejarah Syiah Zaidiyah:**

*   **Kemunculan:** Syiah Zaidiyah muncul pada abad ke-8 Masehi, mengikuti ajaran Zayd bin Ali, cucu dari Husain bin Ali [1, 6]. Zayd bin Ali dikenal sebagai seorang alim yang saleh dan pemberani yang melakukan pemberontakan melawan kekhalifahan Umayyah yang dianggapnya tiran dan korup [2, 6].
*   **Imam Zaid bin Ali:** Zayd bin Ali lahir antara tahun 75-80 Hijriyah. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) Ia belajar dari Imam Muhammad bin Al-Hasan dan kakaknya, Imam Muhammad Al-Baqir. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) Imam Abu Hanifah juga mengakui kecerdasan Imam Zaid [4].
*   **Perkembangan Awal:** Pengikut Zayd mengagumi keberanian, pengetahuan, dan komitmennya pada prinsip-prinsip Islam [6]. Setelah kematian Zayd, pengikutnya terus menjunjung tinggi ajarannya, membentuk mazhab Zaidiyah [6]. [thesubmitters](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)
*   **Yaman:** Zaidiyah memiliki sejarah panjang di Yaman dan memainkan peran penting dalam lanskap politik negara tersebut [5, 6]. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [thesubmitters](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) Yahya Hamiduddin berhasil memisahkan Yaman dari kekuasaan Turki dan mendirikan negara Zaidiyah hingga tahun 1962 [12]. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2)
*   **Perubahan:** Syiah Zaidiyah mengalami perubahan dalam perjalanannya [4]. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) [nu](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-3)

**Doktrin Syiah Zaidiyah:**

*   **Imamah:** Zaidiyah memiliki pandangan yang berbeda tentang Imamah dibandingkan dengan kelompok Syiah lainnya. Mereka percaya bahwa Imamah harus dipegang oleh keturunan Ali dan Fatimah yang memiliki pengetahuan dan integritas moral [6]. [thesubmitters](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) Tidak seperti Syiah lainnya, Zaidiyah tidak membatasi Imamah pada sejumlah pemimpin tertentu dan menerima kemungkinan beberapa keturunan yang memenuhi syarat mengklaim kepemimpinan [6].
*   **Kriteria Imam:** Zaidiyah berpendapat bahwa Imam haruslah keturunan Nabi Muhammad yang paling berpengetahuan dalam ilmu agama [1]. Imam juga tidak harus tetap menjadi Imam seumur hidup [1]. [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
*   **Ijtihad dan Qiyas:** Dalam doktrinnya, Zaidiyah lebih dekat dengan Sunni daripada Syiah lainnya [1]. Mereka memprioritaskan ijtihad (penalaran) dan qiyas (analogi) dalam jurisprudensi daripada kepatuhan dan mistisisme [1]. [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
*   **Khuruj:** Zaidiyah memiliki konsep *khuruj*, di mana *sayyid* Zaidiyah (keturunan Nabi Muhammad) dapat bangkit menjadi pemimpin jika mereka lebih adil dan saleh dari pemimpin yang ada [1]. Sejak pertengahan abad ke-20, ulama Zaidiyah menafsirkan *khuruj* sebagai partisipasi dalam politik elektoral [1]. [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
*   **Rasionalisme:** Zaidiyah menggabungkan prinsip-prinsip rasionalis dan menekankan peran akal dalam memahami teologi dan hukum [6]. Mereka selaras dengan aliran pemikiran Muktazilah dalam fokusnya pada kehendak bebas dan keadilan [6]. [thesubmitters](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)
*   **Keadilan dan Aktivisme:** Zaidiyah menjunjung tinggi pentingnya keadilan sosial dan kewajiban untuk menentang tirani [6]. [thesubmitters](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) Mereka menekankan tindakan langsung melawan tirani [5].
*   **Tidak Maksum:** Zaidiyah tidak percaya pada kemaksuman imam mereka dan tidak menganggap mereka memiliki kualitas supranatural apa pun [2, 13]. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5) Mereka menolak gagasan *nash* imamah yang terdapat dalam Syiah Imamiyah dan Syiah Ismailiyah [13]. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5)
*   **Posisi terhadap Abu Bakar dan Umar:** Imam Zaid menentang pandangan Syiah lain yang menganggap Khalifah Abu Bakar dan Umar sebagai perampas kekuasaan [4]. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) Namun, beberapa kelompok dalam Zaidiyah menolak kepemimpinan Abu Bakar dan Umar [7]. [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6)
*   **Pilar Islam:** Syiah Zaidiyah mengikuti rukun Islam yang sama dengan Muslim lainnya, tetapi dengan penekanan tambahan pada penghormatan kepada para Imam sebagai teladan spiritual [3]. [biblehub](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7)
* **Perbedaan dengan Syiah Imamiyah (Itsna Asyariyah):** Zaidiyah tidak meyakini Imam Ghaib yang akan datang kembali seperti yang diyakini oleh Syiah Itsna Asyariyah [18]. [suaraislam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8)

Penting untuk dicatat bahwa terdapat berbagai pandangan dan interpretasi dalam Syiah Zaidiyah, dan tidak semua kelompok Zaidiyah memiliki pandangan yang sama [7]. [penerbitdaarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-9)


--- Research Result 3 ---
Syiah Itsna Asyariyah, juga dikenal sebagai Syiah Imamiyah atau Syiah Dua Belas Imam, adalah cabang terbesar dalam Islam Syiah, meliputi sekitar 85% dari seluruh Muslim Syiah. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)

**Sejarah Singkat:**

*   **Asal Mula:** Kata "Syiah" secara bahasa berarti "kelompok" atau "pengikut." Dalam terminologi Islam, Syiah merujuk pada kelompok yang menganggap Ali bin Abi Thalib dan keturunannya sebagai Imam dan pemimpin umat setelah Nabi Muhammad SAW. [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Perkembangan Awal:** Syiah muncul sebagai kekuatan politik sejak kasus Shiffin. [uin-malang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) Perselisihan mengenai siapa yang berhak menduduki kekhalifahan setelah Rasulullah SAW wafat mulai tampak setelah Ali r.a. [uin-malang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) membaiat Abu Bakar hingga berakhirnya pemerintahan Umar bin Khattab. [uin-malang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2)
*   **Dinasti Safawi:** Pada awal abad ke-16, berdirinya Kerajaan Safawi di Iran menandai perubahan penting. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) Shah Ismail I menjadikan Syiah Itsna Asyariyah sebagai keyakinan resmi kerajaan. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) Saat itu, pengaruh Syiah di Iran masih terbatas. [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4)
*   **Perkembangan di Indonesia:** Menurut Jalaluddin Rahmat, perkembangan Syiah di Indonesia terbagi dalam empat fase, termasuk masuknya Islam ke Indonesia, meningkatnya popularitas setelah Revolusi Iran 1979, masuknya paham Syiah ke ranah fikih pada 1998, dan pembentukan organisasi seperti IJABI pada tahun 2000. [kompas](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5)

**Doktrin dan Keyakinan:**

*   **Imamah:** Doktrin sentral dalam Syiah Itsna Asyariyah adalah Imamah, yang menyatakan bahwa kepemimpinan spiritual dan politik setelah Nabi Muhammad SAW adalah hak khusus Ali bin Abi Thalib dan keturunannya. [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [kompas](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) Mereka percaya bahwa para Imam memiliki pengetahuan dan otoritas ilahi (Ismat). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
*   **Dua Belas Imam:** Syiah Itsna Asyariyah meyakini adanya dua belas Imam dari Ahlul Bait yang merupakan pemimpin yang sah bagi umat Muslim. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) Urutan Imam tersebut adalah:
    1.  Ali bin Abi Thalib [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [rewangrencang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [kompas](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5)
    2.  Hasan bin Ali [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [rewangrencang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)
    3.  Husain bin Ali
    4.  Ali bin Husain (Ali Zainal Abidin) [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
    5.  Muhammad bin Ali (Muhammad al-Baqir)
    6.  Ja'far bin Muhammad (Ja'far ash-Shadiq) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
    7.  Musa bin Ja'far (Musa al-Kadzim) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
    8.  Ali bin Musa (Ali ar-Ridha) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
    9.  Muhammad bin Ali (Muhammad al-Jawad atau Muhammad at-Taqi) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
    10. Ali bin Muhammad (Ali al-Hadi) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0)
    11. Hasan bin Ali (Hasan al-Askari) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
    12. Muhammad bin Hasan (Muhammad al-Mahdi) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
*   **Rukun Iman:** Syiah Itsna Asyariyah meyakini lima rukun utama, yaitu:
    1.  Tauhid (keesaan Allah) [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
    2.  Adl (keadilan Allah)
    3.  Nubuwwah (kenabian)
    4.  Imamah (kepemimpinan Imam) [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
    5.  Ma'ad (hari kiamat) [rewangrencang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)
*   **Keadilan Tuhan:** Syiah Itsna Asyariyah meyakini bahwa Allah wajib berlaku adil dan keadilan-Nya menuntut adanya Imamah. [rewangrencang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)
*   **Al-Mahdi:** Mereka percaya pada Imam Mahdi yang akan datang untuk menegakkan keadilan dan keamanan setelah bumi dipenuhi dengan kerusakan. [uin-malang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) Imam Mahdi diyakini sebagai Imam ke-12, Muhammad bin Hasan, yang menghilang dan akan kembali pada akhir zaman.
*   **Taqiyah:** Taqiyah adalah tindakan menyembunyikan keyakinan karena takut akan penganiayaan.

**Perbedaan dengan Sunni:**

*   **Imamah:** Perbedaan utama terletak pada konsep Imamah. [scribd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [uin-malang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) Sunni tidak meyakini Imamah sebagai bagian dari rukun iman dan tidak mengkhususkan kepemimpinan hanya pada keturunan Nabi Muhammad SAW.
*   **Sahabat Nabi:** Syiah memiliki pandangan berbeda tentang beberapa sahabat Nabi Muhammad SAW. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
*   **Sumber Hukum:** Syiah memiliki sumber hukum yang berbeda dengan Sunni, termasuk hadis-hadis dari para Imam Ahlul Bait.

**Isu Kontroversial:**

*   **Taqiyah:** Praktik taqiyah sering disalahpahami dan dianggap sebagai bentuk ketidakjujuran.
*   **Pandangan tentang Sahabat Nabi:** Pandangan Syiah tentang beberapa sahabat Nabi Muhammad SAW sering menjadi sumber ketegangan dengan Sunni.
*   **Ekstremisme:** Beberapa kelompok Syiah ekstrem (Ghulat) memiliki keyakinan yang dianggap menyimpang dari ajaran Islam. [kompas](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5)

Penting untuk dicatat bahwa terdapat upaya dari ulama Syiah dan Sunni untuk menjembatani perbedaan dan meningkatkan persatuan.


--- Research Result 4 ---
Okay, I will conduct targeted Google Searches to gather the most recent, credible information on the legal and theological justifications used by Zaidiyah scholars for the concept of 'khuruj' (rebellion against unjust rulers), and how these justifications have been applied in historical contexts, particularly in Yemen. I will then synthesize the information into a verifiable text artifact.

Based on the search results, here's a synthesis of the legal and theological justifications used by Zaidiyah scholars for the concept of 'khuruj' (rebellion against unjust rulers), and how these justifications have been applied in historical contexts, particularly in Yemen:

**1. [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) Theological and Legal Justifications for *Khuruj***

*   **Core Zaydi Belief:** A central tenet of Zaydism is the ethical and legal obligation for Muslims to rise up and depose unjust leaders, including unrighteous sultans and caliphs. [redzambala](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) Rebellion against unjust rulers became a central qualification for any legitimate political-spiritual leader in Zaydism. [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [washingtoninstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   **Imam Zayd's Example:** Zayd ibn Ali's revolt against the Umayyad Caliphate, which he viewed as tyrannical and corrupt, serves as a foundational justification. [redzambala](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [umich](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4) Zaydis believe a true Imam must fight against corrupt rulers. [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [redzambala](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) His uprising and martyrdom became a model for Zaydis. [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [washingtoninstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   **Qualities of a Zaydi Imam:** Zaydis believe that an Imam should lead an uprising against injustice and must possess specific qualities: superior religious and worldly knowledge, scrupulousness, sincerity, liberality, courage, and administrative skills. [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) The Imam must be a male descendant of the Prophet Muhammad through al-Hasan and al-Husayn. [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)
*   **Consensus of *Ulama*:** Zaidis believe Imams assume their position through the consensus of the community's *ulama* (religious scholars). [washingtoninstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   ***Ijtihad* and *Qiyas***: Zaydis prioritize jurisprudence through *ijtihad* (reasoning) and *qiyas* (analogy) over strict obedience and mysticism. [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6)
*   **Ethical Imperative:** Zaydi theological literature emphasizes social justice and human responsibility, with political implications that necessitate rising against unjust rulers. [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [redzambala](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2)
*   **Distinction from Other Shia Branches:** Unlike other Shi'a groups, Zaidis extend the Imamate to descendants of both al-Hasan and al-Husayn, insist on the Imam leading an uprising, and deny the existence of a hidden Imam. [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)

**2. [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [iis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7) [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) Historical Applications in Yemen**

*   **Establishment of the Zaydi State:** In 897 CE, al-Hadi ila'l-Haqq Yahya, a descendant of Imam Hasan ibn Ali, founded the Rassid state in Sa'da, Yemen. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) He asserted the religious duty to rise up against injustice, setting the stage for the Zaydi imamate in Yemen. [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)
*   **The Rassid Imamate:** The Rassid Imamate, established in the late 9th century, continued until the mid-20th century (1962 revolution). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) The Zaydis formed a theocratic political structure that survived with intervals until 1962. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-8)
*   ***Khuruj* as a Tool for Leadership Change:** Zaydi *sayyids* (descendants of the Prophet) traditionally rose to leadership by demonstrating themselves as more just and righteous than existing leaders, often through uprisings or rebellions (*khuruj*). [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6)
*   **Post-Imamate Era:** The end of Imam rule in 1962, and the perception that new rulers did not conform to Zaydi principles, led Zaydi scholars to call for the restoration of the imamate, contributing to the North Yemen Civil War (1962-1970). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2)
*   **Houthi Rebellion:** The Houthi movement's uprising against the Yemeni government is rooted in Zaydi traditions of rebelling against unjust rulers. The subsequent suppression and marginalization of Zaydīs in Yemen was a key grievance leading to the Houthi rebellion in the early 21st century as well as the civil war in the 2010s.
 [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6)*   **Modern Interpretations:** Since the mid-20th century, some Zaydi scholars have reinterpreted *khuruj* as achievable through participation in electoral politics.

**3.  [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)Nuances and Contextual Factors**

*   **Conditions for Rebellion:** While *khuruj* is a key principle, it's not an unconditional call to anarchy.  [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)The leader of the rebellion must possess specific qualities, and the decision to revolt likely involves considerations of the community's capacity and potential consequences.
*   **Influence of Mu'tazili Theology:** Zaydi theology is influenced by Mu'tazili thought, emphasizing reason and justice, which informs their views on legitimate governance and the right to rebel.
*   **Comparison to Sunni and Twelver Shi'a Views:** Zaydism differs from Sunni Islam, which generally emphasizes obedience to rulers to maintain social order, and Twelver Shi'ism, which focuses on the awaited return of the hidden Imam.
*   **Internal Divisions:** Historically, there have been different Zaydi sub-sects (e.g., Jarudiyya and Batriyya), which may have had varying views on the application of *khuruj*.
*   **Tribal Dynamics in Yemen:** The tribal structure of Yemen has often intersected with Zaydi political thought, providing a base for mobilization against perceived injustices.
 [clingendael](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9)
It's important to note that interpretations and applications of *khuruj* have varied throughout Zaydi history, influenced by political circumstances and the views of individual scholars.


--- Research Result 5 ---
The key differences in the interpretation and application of Taqiyah (dissimulation) between Shia Zaidiyah and Shia Ithna Ashariyah, and how these differences manifest in their respective legal and social practices, are as follows:

*   **Definition of Taqiyah:** Taqiyah, literally meaning "prudence" or "fear," is a practice of concealing or disguising one's beliefs, convictions, ideas, feelings, opinions, and/or strategies at a time of eminent danger to save oneself from physical and/or mental injury. [wikishia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) It involves presenting outwardly something that differs from what one believes inwardly. [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2)

*   **Zaidiyah View:** Zaidiyah, generally, dismisses religious dissimulation (Taqiyah). Zaydi doctrine rejects core Imami doctrines like the occultation of imams, esoteric interpretations in Quranic exegesis, or the doctrine of dissimulation of one's beliefs (taqiyya). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5)

*   **Ithna Ashariyah View:** Taqiyyah is one of the basic principles of the Ithna-`Ashri Rafidis and is regarded as one of the basic principles of their religion. [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) They view the one who does not practise it as being the same as one who does not pray and consider it obligatory until the hidden imam appears. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) It means presenting outwardly something that is different from what one believes inwardly, as an act of religious devotion. [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)

*   **Circumstances for Practice:**
    *   **Ithna Ashariyah:** Taqiyyah is permissible in situations where life or property are at risk and whereby no danger to religion would occur. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1)
    *   **Ahl as-Sunnah:** Taqiyyah is something to be resorted to when one has no other choice, and it is an extraordinary measure to be used only in times of extreme necessity. [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4)

*   **Manifestation in Legal and Social Practices:**
    *   **Ithna Ashariyah:** Judges should be chosen by the imam, and according to Twelver belief, one should not accept judges chosen by political authorities unless it is necessary and under conditions that necessitate taqīyah "dissimulation."
 [encyclopedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7)    *   **Zaidiyah:** The Zaidis are known for their political activism
 [aslcinstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8)

Zaidiyah tidak percaya pada kemaksuman imam mereka dan tidak menganggap mereka memiliki kualitas supranatural apa pun [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHrKeFiTZZUYIkProA_Hb_CNgR1BZ3qpABK8mGlClB1BwG5P09tZ4DXajKsvOtE0nl14_-XAIsrIDkgJO81VrzdPwbxCUoZBjQZ9vh-Y8THiQ-cWnQLzCKOSsIcI7yRkbH4).\n\n**2. Syiah diperkenankan mencaci-maki sahabat [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI).\n*   **Syiah Zaidiyah:** Memiliki pandangan yang lebih lunak terhadap para sahabat [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGRQ7r5HBPWz4gfGWEOPM3NI-50bLvbQ6fEF46eUOwcW2-e2I6IxhysdhWpfLJuYS0y-yOlxdyfqLYtAu-KjbUqMPa62ZdrrPK1WuVRTGqTnf8-Ah_gIH7deGLBbgulTTPJXKV1DyFOGjoa3WEgIpo4vRORct-PQEhAMVGrWK_i0z-tlDFUCRvURMjZUNexm4QHHB4kktv9Asbug0a6tQ==). Imam Zaid bin Ali menolak mencela Abu Bakar dan Umar, bahkan memuji mereka [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGRQ7r5HBPWz4gfGWEOPM3NI-50bLvbQ6fEF46eUOwcW2-e2I6IxhysdhWpfLJuYS0y-yOlxdyfqLYtAu-KjbUqMPa62ZdrrPK1WuVRTGqTnf8-Ah_gIH7deGLBbgulTTPJXKV1DyFOGjoa3WEgIpo4vRORct-PQEhAMVGrWK_i0z-tlDFUCRvURMjZUNexm4QHHB4kktv9Asbug0a6tQ==) [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQG-RAOU-Oi8KEUlQNenoGLFX-KD74Q4Jau4-gKpSOyO2SyQkc6I9dWaCki9RWLOWF6fdxqMuTLBe_GuK6RnUyrICCU_rlauSx-jGUroI4DNah7EiL26Iky5eVFWFe2xGp0GCNtz3GSqdn93lEDs9k5DoCbKwfnOeC6fz-eNqxdVbLuARW3reu4wDaCh9mAh560TM9Aj083YZYaMbyA=). Namun, beberapa kelompok dalam Zaidiyah menolak kepemimpinan Abu Bakar dan Umar [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQE7CEBG8uIuWndbZgDEW7iMzYN6x21rTdBY0ZE2e6NBCZ8a7bJC0U4KEq120bS37bfeG4Ou7A4-hSs5wfL5tpiLB0WkxW2rBXKZHzxSwcayui4cCF_b1LTrhWSe4eGhkOEIrBmBOvN36owGEmQ8lyAfxyYiuMsYCJ_IQnc3ebLNEsKZsg==).\n\n**3. Sumber Hukum:**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Al-Qur'an dan Sunnah Nabi (yang diriwayatkan oleh para sahabat secara luas) adalah sumber hukum utama [detik](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF4WLTg-8fFFzx3DEdhGuwvb4H7jGoC50o5PIMIbGb3TPufg3kWbQ86xOd62NvSPtMVTU62x2-JwVLru-sN3AoBJMKAIIdSqmgB9JrbiBmx7-EE4918ZREGiAblx6BqJS4gZuzOCkXBEJwCKWJ4PwLdJ6JDHEyCNE0GSZlis6TRAYxJw45Yj5_VCat1Sxh2DGHl-BqSnwKSrSlBALiRLsMLUyP4blBXAsmqTa4=) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Kitab-kitab hadis utama adalah Shahih Bukhari, Shahih Muslim, dan lainnya [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQG9W59mqQu5TC9h49_kr5U4pfh_Ffu4KoxzVvu-eNlHrxtQOI8y7yRHHEa_xiw9atXhgzOykKZ4gVvP9QY77uAtITRNu7445lt6XU7ul-fhnOHC7Z2FCSZ2hvIkFeBGQdzK5S96vqnHfVO7ptovpbzSLqk2noD6TK2CXPoqUw33MwWqIRXyxMU=) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==).\n*   **Syiah:** Al-Qur'an dan Sunnah, tetapi lebih menekankan pada riwayat-riwayat dari Ahlul Bait (keluarga Nabi) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Kitab-kitab hadis juga berbeda [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGDhRuIM6L0hWTT04CO9P_8myGYh1YNTUozOSXE8Bd0c-UAwQ81YnNUn7YQViABtIbhcLhRwW5ZUjBgnb_wb7Z6QbyvBpbxavvDQET7oA7GG25PM8D61Nrynq_w_KxSE1dLAE8XKDHy4_CytxL0PH9kk1D1ApHO-ar4UREcDfVQQgLeoiF2QLXBjENOP6oa-ELwaYFCjR7rabDJWaXheHX6totu85U=) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQG9W59mqQu5TC9h49_kr5U4pfh_Ffu4KoxzVvu-eNlHrxtQOI8y7yRHHEa_xiw9atXhgzOykKZ4gVvP9QY77uAtITRNu7445lt6XU7ul-fhnOHC7Z2FCSZ2hvIkFeBGQdzK5S96vqnHfVO7ptovpbzSLqk2noD6TK2CXPoqUw33MwWqIRXyxMU=) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI). Kitab-kitab utama Syiah ada empat: Al-Kaafi, Al-Istibshor, Man Laa Yah Dhuruhu Al Faqih, dan Att-Tahdziib [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Dalam doktrinnya, Zaidiyah lebih dekat dengan Sunni daripada Syiah lainnya [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF7FNqciugjT5TKcJs83BpbjL04H-NUkD7woN1cKUIGlvXWA7hdKOhf0eu3tw5YrlM5pcLc1jP2gCa7zagdoJxvaC_zdZGwTtWi7h1Q4aQfZG1XvNZvCfZUgQd1m0xfEwXiSW_K6Q==). Mereka memprioritaskan *ijtihad* (penalaran) dan *qiyas* (analogi) dalam jurisprudensi daripada kepatuhan dan mistisisme [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF7FNqciugjT5TKcJs83BpbjL04H-NUkD7woN1cKUIGlvXWA7hdKOhf0eu3tw5YrlM5pcLc1jP2gCa7zagdoJxvaC_zdZGwTtWi7h1Q4aQfZG1XvNZvCfZUgQd1m0xfEwXiSW_K6Q==).\n\n**4. Praktik Ibadah:**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Cara salat dan wudhu memiliki tata cara tersendiri yang telah dikenal luas.\n*   **Syiah:** Terdapat perbedaan kecil dalam tata cara salat dan wudhu [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Syiah membolehkan nikah mut'ah (pernikahan sementara), yang dilarang dalam Sunni [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQG9W59mqQu5TC9h49_kr5U4pfh_Ffu4KoxzVvu-eNlHrxtQOI8y7yRHHEa_xiw9atXhgzOykKZ4gVvP9QY77uAtITRNu7445lt6XU7ul-fhnOHC7Z2FCSZ2hvIkFeBGQdzK5S96vqnHfVO7ptovpbzSLqk2noD6TK2CXPoqUw33MwWqIRXyxMU=).\n\n**5. Teologi:**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Rukun Iman ada 6 [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGDhRuIM6L0hWTT04CO9P_8myGYh1YNTUozOSXE8Bd0c-UAwQ81YnNUn7YQViABtIbhcLhRwW5ZUjBgnb_wb7Z6QbyvBpbxavvDQET7oA7GG25PM8D61Nrynq_w_KxSE1dLAE8XKDHy4_CytxL0PH9kk1D1ApHO-ar4UREcDfVQQgLeoiF2QLXBjENOP6oa-ELwaYFCjR7rabDJWaXheHX6totu85U=) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==).\n*   **Syiah:** Rukun agama (*ushuluddin*) ada 5, yaitu Tauhid, Nubuwwah, Imamah, Al Adlu, Al Ma'ad [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [daarulhuda](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGou8Ae0igIzWgVsOt8TpDIX8ZOrwoCNyYz1PjYOJMz8RmzEKDiQ4BGhdFinnNFdwQi6wleJ4wKAivBNLUrALDv_758cLSZvwz9wjJ9XtYOt-44z-ILRM-b9hMKBfsNNsPKbnOIbaRXuggdVocvbt-YiQtdsaiP5FkYaokB0435LLLGJQ==) [rewangrencang](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH8C1icok6EPBavTBndGvz-5H5S-XZkh-sGceR-0n3vybnE8ovKyPl2pUVO2HV82qfN1G6l7oX7jqza0LPXQemXhI4V0kFyEDuFFNi5x2Yc2yyvWo7bIY1EIY1vu9r_8J0cautvEfWaMyOTfph8g6hH7FqcLGc50O2o9RJrpmwawHDGgco=).\n\n**6. Al-Qur'an:**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Meyakini Al-Qur'an yang ada saat ini adalah sama dengan yang diturunkan kepada Nabi Muhammad SAW [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==).\n*   **Syiah:** Sebagian ulama Syiah meyakini bahwa Al-Qur'an mereka berbeda dengan Al-Qur'an Sunni, meskipun ada juga yang menyatakan sama (tetapi berbeda dalam penafsiran) [persis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGDhRuIM6L0hWTT04CO9P_8myGYh1YNTUozOSXE8Bd0c-UAwQ81YnNUn7YQViABtIbhcLhRwW5ZUjBgnb_wb7Z6QbyvBpbxavvDQET7oA7GG25PM8D61Nrynq_w_KxSE1dLAE8XKDHy4_CytxL0PH9kk1D1ApHO-ar4UREcDfVQQgLeoiF2QLXBjENOP6oa-ELwaYFCjR7rabDJWaXheHX6totu85U=) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==) [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI).\n\n**7. Raj'ah (Kebangkitan Kembali):**\n\n*   **Sunni:** Tidak ada dalam ajaran Ahlussunnah [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI).\n*   **Syiah:** Raj'ah adalah salah satu aqidah Syiah, di mana di akhir zaman, Imam Mahdi akan keluar dan ahlul bait akan membalas dendam kepada musuh-musuhnya [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Zaidiyah tidak meyakini Imam Ghaib yang akan datang kembali seperti yang diyakini oleh Syiah Itsna Asyariyah [suaraislam](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFmP88-rpL1neCRPRF3GqG1HE8sLxII8U44PJ01F_pKffmF6bqhgDM0gciBUBtnGGnOfUZ6jCDLkh0RJwns2vXnCcXgjwFziF_nevBbZGZw7drZ0BTng3A2JLUNV1Y0iQPYWM01HmEU-8MO).\n\n**8. Taqiyah (Menyembunyikan Keyakinan):**\n\n*   **Syiah:** Diperbolehkan menyembunyikan keyakinan untuk melindungi diri [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Zaidiyah, umumnya, menolak *taqiyah* [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGtFP9P05wY6G4hh69C2zLutWalSzgjMGoGJ-dstm_-WzkKnBK0qZZ4Hhn39xLc9oGn1cN7BLTEZ-_onqkKTIEvhqYDIN5wqspOBKZRKb3zqNol0oOR5jpGEB2DCzAjDf7n3B3_qOja9fDto8QdWNS1Wgg=). Sementara itu, bagi  Ithna Ashariyah, *taqiyah* adalah salah satu prinsip dasar dan dianggap wajib sampai imam yang tersembunyi muncul [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGInp7C8N1hwkkl2eJ5MoyFgCzV-oNlVlBnMKC0iEucWBiazlK6CQqlnmlPahZ0UhmZALwC4wQRE4jW1lmUdCcWElhVdDe0Tqt62HTlqml7Z5FSSxxQAhQ43uAC-MVpIXF-) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHX1Y7hmT4vI_tuGQJeFTsmuiq6ne8oUBsXyjHej3RJqbaxIVEyNIlf5cKhrAhKICaojjp1d-FbmgNbOoIgdEvPH9z0lZVXVc3WG-O0w9_IBNziRyR64akEvyYKq5N5Phz8Apk-B7Ut15dh3PNbZe3S7QmIN8-UwGfy8ytsANY6yNDnbixjbhq-fr4wuUvkjg==).\n\n**9. Pandangan Terhadap Pemimpin yang Tidak Adil dan Konsep *Khuruj*:**\n\n*   **Zaidiyah:** Memandang bolehnya memberontak terhadap pemimpin yang jahat [iainkudus](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQGJ0rI2oCPL26lXVWVeZNhrimCf44NBuY1OtOk0LXkj9WNw5yyC4P6xElfu0Sb8FBd3pgARMuVDFTw5TdxCIe3nZsKDupXO6zoJ1Cal2zNS7xQkz_rQ9c21JHeMOuV2A6yQyh1ubKIvHUTmRHkg_hvm9us_fEFOsm-kQl_f_kJBccsT1UmkHP2r-gbPoCoI) [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). Ini adalah inti dari konsep *khuruj*. Zaydis percaya bahwa seorang Imam sejati harus berjuang melawan penguasa yang korup [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHTFVjjrTzI1FmKuoihOLXnGvJ7vShVzXXwUjN2Fi3UcGggevIxvy6ZBgRejRUiyOzNBCCNtDwY5XJypE1veEe79HmL9MSFx_HCzhHE1RguF5aKCftrfxBhqJ73hYk08_RUbmttTC0tvPDhXnIgnehoDu1WUcs4) [redzambala](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHk2m32VMkJMa3KWeoQP-GZ2TY6Vk50sTN-ip-P4KJ2MtmG4PHeUGo4V03jq1YJA1213ob9im2D4Oj9oYRpPpSnTys2EPJ2-alLwZ2aGkFdAa-QgAYoNQBj-3mJjP3MrqRwZGa3s3_JA6yXXj8J5djqL7w=) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQE7lDs8s5XQQQpkxbk06sYIwuIZZh7vwXDWe9HpSgVnmSQ8_VSC7dcx07TOPlVr4lofeq3vUOsFiVQgeexOJgdiINK9sMZxJfY-q2Htx2C8wTsErbXYY3koz1ZTZSMmIrQ=). Pemberontakan melawan penguasa yang tidak adil menjadi kualifikasi utama bagi setiap pemimpin spiritual-politik yang sah dalam Zaydism [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHTFVjjrTzI1FmKuoihOLXnGvJ7vShVzXXwUjN2Fi3UcGggevIxvy6ZBgRejRUiyOzNBCCNtDwY5XJypE1veEe79HmL9MSFx_HCzhHE1RguF5aKCftrfxBhqJ73hYk08_RUbmttTC0tvPDhXnIgnehoDu1WUcs4) [washingtoninstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFtLmeY78mTVFzCYF9e-wjxIPGNRttxrEnesYpwP03HtRxl-2DOl1uGPLL7aqv4I7zz8jQ0vAekLuIqf7eSnSzbadXo6Jedm2Sig5sZPV7MPu4WnKxFyCUz4wkR2I1bsWxYc0k3s84YwTRSzwJwikUF6TmOH0LoXXe4HB-CTW_xzanUUONV7UD_oa9oh4wsWnKFyfA6Sw==). Sejak pertengahan abad ke-20, ulama Zaidiyah menafsirkan *khuruj* sebagai partisipasi dalam politik elektoral [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF7FNqciugjT5TKcJs83BpbjL04H-NUkD7woN1cKUIGlvXWA7hdKOhf0eu3tw5YrlM5pcLc1jP2gCa7zagdoJxvaC_zdZGwTtWi7h1Q4aQfZG1XvNZvCfZUgQd1m0xfEwXiSW_K6Q==).\n\n**Sejarah dan Perkembangan Syiah Zaidiyah:**\n\nSyiah Zaidiyah muncul pada abad ke-8 Masehi, mengikuti ajaran Zayd bin Ali [1, 6]. Zayd bin Ali dikenal sebagai seorang alim yang saleh dan pemberani yang melakukan pemberontakan melawan kekhalifahan Umayyah yang dianggapnya tiran dan korup [2, 6]. Zaidiyah memiliki sejarah panjang di Yaman dan memainkan peran penting dalam lanskap politik negara tersebut [5, 6] [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQFxZYDVkQ9XT328mO_-xJeJo1iqAsh_uB0-gRcLCHsvUhM-xsp8qZWGJkmi54Rf1gai2DJYb4tIoBHdXTHCcHeYl6xFyL0aI3Itc3eSDrc87o3qgkUjqSTN-8poTVYuit0Yix9R4Waz74k2ohqejZgh90u2FFYJCz_CwmucVDInje7fnDBRDsfuTkbTxyPBTLKecFf0MnuK9tehPXvC41kT_ixoXKRFmJ2rJTjMRPQdpMxUYaplqMM=) [thesubmitters](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH7aHK9JTDa0zUSQrF_-Kz6rsOXZHrn3R2QzPKMeW2NCgcj17hNRDhvMwjcPG_oWbDhfPbNgN7qGrdJDXXa4ENgEC0JZA8JmK8D82I1b2EmlbcxYJ5WyIhR3Kk-KiaRp7QqBWOlQQ==).\n\n**Sejarah dan Perkembangan Syiah Itsna Asyariyah:**\n\nPada awal abad ke-16, berdirinya Kerajaan Safawi di Iran menandai perubahan penting [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQEKYz28Z5PAZPLQIzpRzT0iH3cBS9cR9b8dXX0N8MJ6r7YvRS4UnSb7batBzFFADqpf_dyWuvDEbg9NSKo1VUHalu8dTRsnN_lLexCfHX77nUiEDmLBkqWsixngSHC1cdv67tu7Ycu2J_x3GE7w7q1BJ1fdWx2oSjstlZJDhsB6AEnQVLh5T9B3ER_tM1eQks8CzhZUH55-PWxfFHOTWlIuj2F5pgJv6jExZ2jOkoOs7LnYfp05zmYBsso=). Shah Ismail I menjadikan Syiah Itsna Asyariyah sebagai keyakinan resmi kerajaan [hidayatullah](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQER30xoRAolCOcmex9bzWgS8XaV7L3ZYM_Jdl63onH9xZyQBZIpXGszdoGgCUX9l-o51nzyp3F-tIIEUAzl0cb-8z_E5eulCZxTthM-1vZA2ZYfRQ2MggvWEL20LVuxWu67jR5G7n-I2-2T5PWu-z6oan5cHfOgChIYCcVi8AbPppvHhaJ-yRxE4qsL6lZv8TjJWBl9e67sm--5ZqdILRRPTr3s6vhW6SV7).\n\nPenting untuk diingat bahwa perbedaan-perbedaan ini seringkali menjadi sumber ketegangan antara Sunni dan Syiah [liputan6](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQH4TL1DMnLBjX5a8QBvZtGMm0wgkOyC4vtL_B4Q1cPfDjV_VWLLbA0UfErQ-AS6srxSUv7LP1yQ_tSmbgeWBBuV_oOh6sZrn6q_DfDcnn2Il5hmBFymrxTvOAFljD8Ouunmdfyehn61hWgjj7upKcqi2H0I2In1pqawDwOhaxwW24xvP6iSUErQPnxSSkJRstPTMgdQ-HKiUNkP_jYngAWXlIaJCcuxu3Vzeg==). [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) Theological and Legal Justifications for *Khuruj***\n\n*   **Core Zaydi Belief:** A central tenet of Zaydism is the ethical and legal obligation for Muslims to rise up and depose unjust leaders, including unrighteous sultans and caliphs. [redzambala](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) Rebellion against unjust rulers became a central qualification for any legitimate political-spiritual leader in Zaydism. [redzambala](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [umich](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4) Zaydis believe a true Imam must fight against corrupt rulers. [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [washingtoninstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)\n*   **Qualities of a Zaydi Imam:** Zaydis believe that an Imam should lead an uprising against injustice and must possess specific qualities: superior religious and worldly knowledge, scrupulousness, sincerity, liberality, courage, and administrative skills. [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) The Imam must be a male descendant of the Prophet Muhammad through al-Hasan and al-Husayn. [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)\n*   **Consensus of *Ulama*:** Zaidis believe Imams assume their position through the consensus of the community's *ulama* (religious scholars). [washingtoninstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)\n*   ***Ijtihad* and *Qiyas***: Zaydis prioritize jurisprudence through *ijtihad* (reasoning) and *qiyas* (analogy) over strict obedience and mysticism. [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6)\n*   **Ethical Imperative:** Zaydi theological literature emphasizes social justice and human responsibility, with political implications that necessitate rising against unjust rulers. [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [redzambala](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2)\n*   **Distinction from Other Shia Branches:** Unlike other Shi'a groups, Zaidis extend the Imamate to descendants of both al-Hasan and al-Husayn, insist on the Imam leading an uprising, and deny the existence of a hidden Imam. [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)\n\n**2. [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) [iis](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7) [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) Historical Applications in Yemen**\n\n*   **Establishment of the Zaydi State:** In 897 CE, al-Hadi ila'l-Haqq Yahya, a descendant of Imam Hasan ibn Ali, founded the Rassid state in Sa'da, Yemen. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) He asserted the religious duty to rise up against injustice, setting the stage for the Zaydi imamate in Yemen. [saet](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5)\n*   **The Rassid Imamate:** The Rassid Imamate, established in the late 9th century, continued until the mid-20th century (1962 revolution). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) The Zaydis formed a theocratic political structure that survived with intervals until 1962. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-8)\n*   ***Khuruj* as a Tool for Leadership Change:** Zaydi *sayyids* (descendants of the Prophet) traditionally rose to leadership by demonstrating themselves as more just and righteous than existing leaders, often through uprisings or rebellions (*khuruj*). [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6)\n*   **Post-Imamate Era:** The end of Imam rule in 1962, and the perception that new rulers did not conform to Zaydi principles, led Zaydi scholars to call for the restoration of the imamate, contributing to the North Yemen Civil War (1962-1970). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2)\n*   **Houthi Rebellion:** The Houthi movement's uprising against the Yemeni government is rooted in Zaydi traditions of rebelling against unjust rulers. The subsequent suppression and marginalization of Zaydīs in Yemen was a key grievance leading to the Houthi rebellion in the early 21st century as well as the civil war in the 2010s.\n [britannica](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6)*   **Modern Interpretations:** Since the mid-20th century, some Zaydi scholars have reinterpreted *khuruj* as achievable through participation in electoral politics.\n\n**3.  [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)Nuances and Contextual Factors**\n\n*   **Conditions for Rebellion:** While *khuruj* is a key principle, it's not an unconditional call to anarchy.  [umt](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)The leader of the rebellion must possess specific qualities, and the decision to revolt likely involves considerations of the community's capacity and potential consequences.\n*   **Influence of Mu'tazili Theology:** Zaydi theology is influenced by Mu'tazili thought, emphasizing reason and justice, which informs their views on legitimate governance and the right to rebel.\n*   **Comparison to Sunni and Twelver Shi'a Views:** Zaydism differs from Sunni Islam, which generally emphasizes obedience to rulers to maintain social order, and Twelver Shi'ism, which focuses on the awaited return of the hidden Imam.\n*   **Internal Divisions:** Historically, there have been different Zaydi sub-sects (e.g., Jarudiyya and Batriyya), which may have had varying views on the application of *khuruj*.\n*   **Tribal Dynamics in Yemen:** The tribal structure of Yemen has often intersected with Zaydi political thought, providing a base for mobilization against perceived injustices.\n [clingendael](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9)\nIt's important to note that interpretations and applications of *khuruj* have varied throughout Zaydi history, influenced by political circumstances and the views of individual scholars.\n",
    "The key differences in the interpretation and application of Taqiyah (dissimulation) between Shia Zaidiyah and Shia Ithna Ashariyah, and how these differences manifest in their respective legal and social practices, are as follows:\n\n*   **Definition of Taqiyah:** Taqiyah, literally meaning \"prudence\" or \"fear,\" is a practice of concealing or disguising one's beliefs, convictions, ideas, feelings, opinions, and/or strategies at a time of eminent danger to save oneself from physical and/or mental injury. [wikishia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-0) [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2) It involves presenting outwardly something that differs from what one believes inwardly. [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-2)\n\n*   **Zaidiyah View:** Zaidiyah, generally, dismisses religious dissimulation (Taqiyah). Zaydi doctrine rejects core Imami doctrines like the occultation of imams, esoteric interpretations in Quranic exegesis, or the doctrine of dissimulation of one's beliefs (taqiyya). [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-5)\n\n*   **Ithna Ashariyah View:** Taqiyyah is one of the basic principles of the Ithna-`Ashri Rafidis and is regarded as one of the basic principles of their religion. [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) They view the one who does not practise it as being the same as one who does not pray and consider it obligatory until the hidden imam appears. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-6) [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) It means presenting outwardly something that is different from what one believes inwardly, as an act of religious devotion. [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3)\n\n*   **Circumstances for Practice:**\n    *   **Ithna Ashariyah:** Taqiyyah is permissible in situations where life or property are at risk and whereby no danger to religion would occur. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-1)\n    *   **Ahl as-Sunnah:** Taqiyyah is something to be resorted to when one has no other choice, and it is an extraordinary measure to be used only in times of extreme necessity. [islamqa](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-3) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-4)\n\n*   **Manifestation in Legal and Social Practices:**\n    *   **Ithna Ashariyah:** Judges should be chosen by the imam, and according to Twelver belief, one should not accept judges chosen by political authorities unless it is necessary and under conditions that necessitate taqīyah \"dissimulation.\"\n [encyclopedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-7)    *   **Zaidiyah:** The Zaidis are known for their political activism\n [aslcinstitute](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/4-8)\n"
